<article id="post-2142" class="post-2142 page type-page status-publish has-post-thumbnail infinite-scroll-item" itemtype="https://schema.org/CreativeWork" itemscope>
	<div class="inside-article">
		
		<div class="entry-content" itemprop="text">
			
<h2 class="wp-block-heading front-h2">Who We Are</h2>



<p><u>We are a team of doctors and psychologists</u> with a comprehensive approach to mental, emotional, and behavioral issues in children and adolescents.</p>



<p><u>Our goal</u> is to shift the focus from your child&#8217;s &#8220;misconduct&#8221; to what that conduct may signal.</p>



<p><u>Our mission</u> is to help you and your child navigate the challenges you face, and to optimize your child&#8217;s psychological and emotional well-being.</p>



<p>We want your child to thrive.<span style="width: 100%;"></span></p>



<div class="wp-block-columns has-5-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow"><div class="wp-block-image authorAvatars">
<figure class="aligncenter is-resized"><a href="/author/drlangham/"><img width="185" height="185" decoding="async" src="/wp-content/uploads/2019/01/ree-langham.png" alt="Dr. Ree Langham" style="width:150px" title="ree langham"></a></figure></div>


<p class="has-text-align-center"><strong>Ree Langham, Ph.D.</strong></p>



<p class="has-text-align-center has-normal-font-size">Child and family psychologist with over a decade of experience. Dr. Langham writes about ADHD and anxiety.</p>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow"><div class="wp-block-image authorAvatars">

<h2 class="wp-block-heading front-h2">How to Get Help for Your Child</h2>



<div class="wp-block-columns has-3-columns is-layout-flex wp-container-core-columns-is-layout-9d6595d7 wp-block-columns-is-layout-flex">
<div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img width="1000" height="666" decoding="async" src="https://parentingpod.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/boy-therapy.jpg" alt="Boy at Assessment" title="boy therapy"></figure>



<p class="has-text-align-center"><strong><strong>Tests &amp; Assessments</strong></strong></p>



<p class="has-text-align-center">What to expect from the tests physicians and psychologists most frequently use to evaluate your child&#8217;s behavior. Find out how these assessments are utilized to diagnose ADHD, <a style="outline: none; display: inline-block;" href="/self-evaluation-checklist-students-with-autism/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">autism</a>,&nbsp;<a href="/anxiety-checklist-for-kids/">anxiety</a>,&nbsp;<a href="" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">depression</a>, anger management, emotional issues, and more.</p>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img width="1000" height="667" decoding="async" src="https://parentingpod.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/teen-therapy.jpg" alt="Teen in Therapy" title="teen therapy"></figure>



<p class="has-text-align-center"><strong>Treatments &amp; Therapies</strong></p>



<p class="has-text-align-center">No single type of therapy works for everyone. We explain what the options are, what questions to ask, and what to keep in mind when choosing among them. Once treatment is underway, you will also find out what you can do to help it succeed.</p>
</div>



<div class="wp-block-column is-layout-flow wp-block-column-is-layout-flow">
<figure class="wp-block-image"><img width="1000" height="667" decoding="async" src="https://parentingpod.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/11/boy-spinner.jpg" alt="Boy With Spinner" title="boy spinner"></figure>



<p class="has-text-align-center"><strong>Product Safety &amp; Reviews</strong></p>



<p class="has-text-align-center">Many companies claim their products improve behavior and&nbsp;mental health.&nbsp;We explain what the research shows, and we share the results our own clients have had with&nbsp;<a style="outline: none; display: inline-block;" href="/best-weighted-blanket-for-kids/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">weighted blankets</a>,&nbsp;<a style="outline: none; display: inline-block;" href="/best-kids-trampoline/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">trampolines</a>,&nbsp;<a href="/best-fidget-spinner-cube/" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">spinners</a>, and more.</p>
</div>
</div>
